Disadvantages: The hotel management is problematic and the service is too poor. I checked in on the first day of the Chinese New Year. The room is far from the front desk, and it takes at least ten minutes to go back and forth. In addition, the hot water is not hot enough, and I almost caught a cold when taking a shower. The hotel is outside the city, and it is a bit far to go into the city for meals.
